include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_INDEX_VALUE(_tab, _index)           ((_tab)[_index])
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_INDEX_TEST(_tab, _p)                ((_tab)[(_p)->index])
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_INDEX_SET(_tab, _p) {(_tab)[(_p)->index] = 1;}
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_INDEX_CLEAR(_tab, _p) {(_tab)[(_p)->index] = 0;}
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_INDEX_TEST_AND_SET(_tab, _p)        ((_tab)[(_p)->index] == 0 ? ((_tab)[(_p)->index] = 1) : 0)
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_INDEX_IS_SET(_tab, _p)              NMG_INDEX_TEST(_tab, _p)
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_INDEX_FIRST_TIME(_tab, _p)          NMG_INDEX_TEST_AND_SET(_tab, _p)
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_INDEX_ASSIGN(_tab, _p, _val) {(_tab)[(_p)->index] = _val;}
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_INDEX_GET(_tab, _p)                 ((_tab)[(_p)->index])
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_INDEX_GETP(_ty, _tab, _p)           ((struct _ty *)((_tab)[(_p)->index]))
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_INDEX_OR(_tab, _p, _val) {(_tab)[(_p)->index] |= _val;}
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_INDEX_AND(_tab, _p, _val) {(_tab)[(_p)->index] &= _val;}
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_INDEX_RETURN_IF_SET_ELSE_SET(_tab, _index) { ;#define NMG_0MANIFOLD  1
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_1MANIFOLD  2
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_2MANIFOLD  4
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_DANGLING   8 /* NMG_2MANIFOLD + 4th bit for special cond (UNUSED) */
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_3MANIFOLD 16
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_SET_MANIFOLD(_t, _p, _v) NMG_INDEX_OR(_t, _p, _v)
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_MANIFOLDS(_t, _p)        NMG_INDEX_VALUE(_t, (_p)->index)
include/nmg/index.h: #define NMG_CP_MANIFOLD(_t, _p, _q)  (_t)[(_p)->index] = (_t)[(_q)->index]
